											A Sale transaction is used by merchants for the immediate purchase of goods or services. This transaction completes both the authorization and capture in a single transaction request. The Sale transaction is an Authorization and Capture transaction that, if approved, is automatically included in the open batch for settlement.

											Encrypted Sale
										Element:br
											The Clearent Payment Gateway supports the collection of magnetic stripe data using MagTek Secure Card Reader/Authenticators (SCRA) conforming to the MagneSafe V5 specification; examples of such products include the Dynamag (with USB interface to a PC or other device), iDynamo (with Apple 30-pin connector on an iPhone/iPad), or uDynamo (with audio jack interface to a mobile device).
										Element:p
											The entire responseData object returned by the MagTek SCRA must be included in the encrypted-track-data field; previous versions of this API spec had erroneously indicated that only the encrypted Track2 object was required. You must piece together the responses from the SDK to create a string similar to the code sample provided.

									Node:

											Sale Unencrypted
										Element:br
											Sending of unencrypted Track2 data should only be used when the following conditions are in place:
										Element:ul
										Element:li
											When a secure Card Reader product is used at the point of sale, such as a MagTek SCRA or an equivalent product from another vendor. Simply capturing the track data with a non-encrypting card reader exposes the merchant to significant risk of compromise, and will not be permitted.
										Element:li
											The Transaction API request originator has implemented their own mechanism for decrypting the track data, securely storing it, and protecting it from compromise according to PCI-DSS and/or PA-DSS requirements.
										Element:li
											When the track data decryption and storage mechanism has been subjected to a qualified PCI-DSS or PA-DSS assessment process, and the service provider who manages that operation maintains annual compliance.
										Element:p
											Please discuss your particular situation with your Clearent point of contact to ensure that the use of this option will be permitted.
										Element:br
											Track 2 data should NOT include either the beginning or end sentinel.
